									<b>Total plays:  16665</b><br /><br />Max plays in a month:      1975  (#6)<br />Max players in a month:     700  (#7)<br /><br />Essen 2016 Ranking Tracker Rank:   23<br /><br /><div ><a href="/image/3863072"><img src="https://cf.geekdo-images.com/images/pic3863072_t.png" onload="ImageResizer.resize(this);"></a></div><br /><br />And now we have a large drop in maximum players and plays, although in terms of overall plays this game is very close to Feast for Odin.  Although it has proved to have way less general popularity, the playrate has been remarkably consistent over the year with only minimum drop-off, and also has a relatively high number of plays per player every month, which is how it has come to close to Feast for Odin in overall plays.  The lowest game on the ranking tracker to make the Top 10 in plays.<br /><br />

			This geeklist looks at the Essen 2016 releases and ranks them by total plays over the year.  <br /><br />The red line on each graph shows the number of total plays per month, the blue line shows the number of players of the game.  The months are listed as months after Essen, with month 1 being Essen month, October 2016.

			This geeklist looks at the Essen 2016 releases and ranks them by total plays over the year.  <br /><br />The red line on each graph shows the number of total plays per month, the blue line shows the number of players of the game.  The months are listed as months after Essen, with month 1 being Essen month, October 2016.

			This geeklist looks at the Essen 2016 releases and ranks them by total plays over the year.  <br /><br />The red line on each graph shows the number of total plays per month, the blue line shows the number of players of the game.  The months are listed as months after Essen, with month 1 being Essen month, October 2016.
